    tsurai
   </i>
   )
  </li>
 </ul>

     よう
    </a>
   </span>
   – volitional ending [う for
   <i>
    u
   </i>
   -verbs, よう for
   <i>
    ru
   </i>
   -verbs]: "Let's…" or "I will" (
   <i>
    u
   </i>
   ,
   <i>
    yō
   </i>
   )
  </li>
  <li>
   <span class="Jpan" lang="ja">
    <a href="/wiki/%E3%81%9B%E3%82%8B#Japanese" title="せる">
     せる
    </a>
   </span>
   、
   <span class="Jpan" lang="ja">
    <a href="/wiki/%E3%81%95%E3%81%9B%E3%82%8B#Japanese" title="させる">
     させる
    </a>
   </span>
   – causative ending [せる for
   <i>
    u
   </i>
   -verbs, させる for
   <i>
    ru
   </i>
   -verbs]: to make [someone do something], to allow (
   <i>
    seru
   </i>
   ,
   <i>
    saseru
   </i>
   )
  </li>
  <li>
   <span class="Jpan" lang="ja">
    <a href="/wiki/%E3%82%8C%E3%82%8B#Japanese" title="れる">
     れる
    </a>
   </span>
   、
   <span class="Jpan" lang="ja">
    <a href="/wiki/%E3%82%89%E3%82%8C%E3%82%8B#Japanese" title="られる">
     られる
    </a>
   </span>
   – passive verb ending [れる for
   <i>
    u
   </i>
   -verbs, られる for
   <i>
    ru
   </i>
   -verbs]: to be &lt;verbed&gt; [e.g., 食べられる, "to be eaten"]  (
   <i>
    reru
   </i>
   ,
   <i>
    rareru
   </i>
   )
  </li>
  <li>
   <span class="Jpan" lang="ja">
    <a href="/wiki/%E3%81%9D%E3%81%86#Japanese" title="そう">
     そうだ
    </a>
   </span>
   – indicates that it
   <i>
    seems
   </i>
   the verb occurs [e.g., "It seems he ate"] (
   <i>
    sōda
   </i>
   )
  </li>
  <li>
   <span class="Jpan" lang="ja">
    <a href="/wiki/%E3%81%9F#Japanese" title="た">
     た
    </a>
   </span>
   – informal past-tense (
   <i>
    ta
   </i>
   )
  </li>
  <li>
   <span class="Jpan" lang="ja">
    <a href="/wiki/%E3%81%9F%E3%81%84#Japanese" title="たい">
     たい
    </a>
   </span>
   – indicates desire to perform verb (
   <i>
    tai
   </i>
   )
  </li>
  <li>
   <span class="Jpan" lang="ja">
    <a href="/wiki/%E3%81%A0%E3%82%8D%E3%81%86#Japanese" title="だろう">
     だろう
    </a>
   </span>
   – indicates that it
   <i>
    seems
   </i>
   the verb occurs; also used to ask whether the verb occurs (
   <i>
    darō
   </i>
   )
  </li>
  <li>
   <span class="Jpan" lang="ja">
    <a href="/wiki/%E3%81%AA%E3%81%84#Japanese" title="ない">
     ない
    </a>
   </span>
   、
   <span class="Jpan" lang="ja">
    <a href="/wiki/%E3%82%93#Japanese" title="ん">
     ん
    </a>
   </span>
   – informal negative (
   <i>
    nai
   </i>
   ,
   <i>
    n
   </i>
   ) [ん is a slurred version and sounds a little masculine]
  </li>
  <li>
   <span class="Jpan" lang="ja">
    <a href="/wiki/%E3%81%AC#Japanese" title="ぬ">
     ぬ
    </a>
   </span>
   – archaic informal negative ["he hath", "thou didst", etc.] (
   <i>
    nu
   </i>
   )
  </li>
  <li>
   <span class="Jpan" lang="ja">
    <a href="/wiki/%E3%81%BE%E3%81%99#Japanese" title="ます">
     ます
    </a>
   </span>
   – formal non-past ending (
   <i>
    masu
   </i>

  </li>
 </ul>
